Abstract: Residual policy learning (RPL), in which a learned policy refines a static base policy using deep reinforcement learning (DRL), has shown strong performance across various robotic applications. Its effectiveness is particularly evident in autonomous racing, a domain that serves as a challenging benchmark for real-world DRL. However, deploying RPL-based controllers introduces system complexity and increases inference latency. We address this by introducing an extension of RPL named attenuated residual policy optimization ($α$-RPO). Unlike standard RPL, $α$-RPO yields a standalone neural policy by progressively attenuating the base policy, which initially serves to bootstrap learning. Furthermore, this mechanism enables a form of privileged learning, where the base policy is permitted to use sensor modalities not required for final deployment. We design $α$-RPO to integrate seamlessly with PPO, ensuring that the attenuated influence of the base controller is dynamically compensated during policy optimization. We evaluate $α$-RPO by building a framework for 1:10-scaled autonomous racing around it. In both simulation and zero-shot real-world transfer to Roboracer cars, $α$-RPO not only reduces system complexity but also improves driving performance compared to baselines - demonstrating its practicality for robotic deployment. Our code is available at: https://github.com/raphajaner/arpo_racing.

It further employs a semantic-guided soft-label contrastive learning objective to align similar action primitives across tasks, enhancing generalization and motion consistency. An adaptive weighting strategy, inspired by curriculum learning, dynamically balances contrastive and imitation objectives for stable and effective training. ### [311] [From Passive Monitoring to Active Defence: Resilient Control of Manipulators Under Cyberattacks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13003)
*Gabriele Gualandi,Alessandro V. Papadopoulos*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种针对冗余机械臂的主动防御机制，以抵御难以被传统残差检测器（如卡方检验）发现的虚假数据注入攻击（FDIAs），通过引入基于执行器投影、无测量的状态预测器生成异常分数，并据此衰减控制输入，在保证闭环稳定性和名义性能的同时提供概率性保障。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建包含反馈线性化机械臂、稳态卡尔曼滤波器和卡方异常检测器的闭环模型；在此被动监控层基础上，提出一种主动控制级防御机制：利用新型执行器投影、无测量状态预测器生成异常分数，并通过其单调函数衰减控制输入；同时从攻击者角度推导出计算一步最优隐蔽攻击的凸QCQP问题。

Result: 在6自由度平面机械臂上的仿真表明，所提防御方法显著降低攻击引起的末端执行器偏差，且在无攻击时保持正常的任务性能。

Conclusion: 该主动防御架构提升了冗余机械臂对隐蔽FDIAs的鲁棒性，实现了从被动监控到主动防护的范式转变，并提供了名义执行损失的概率保证与闭环稳定性。

Abstract: Cyber-physical robotic systems are vulnerable to false data injection attacks (FDIAs), in which an adversary corrupts sensor signals while evading residual-based passive anomaly detectors such as the chi-squared test. Such stealthy attacks can induce substantial end-effector deviations without triggering alarms. This paper studies the resilience of redundant manipulators to stealthy FDIAs and advances the architecture from passive monitoring to active defence. We formulate a closed-loop model comprising a feedback-linearized manipulator, a steady-state Kalman filter, and a chi-squared-based anomaly detector. Building on this passive monitoring layer, we propose an active control-level defence that attenuates the control input through a monotone function of an anomaly score generated by a novel actuation-projected, measurement-free state predictor. The proposed design provides probabilistic guarantees on nominal actuation loss and preserves closed-loop stability. From the attacker perspective, we derive a convex QCQP for computing one-step optimal stealthy attacks. Simulations on a 6-DOF planar manipulator show that the proposed defence significantly reduces attack-induced end-effector deviation while preserving nominal task performance in the absence of attacks.

*Ruogu Li,Sikai Li,Yao Mu,Mingyu Ding*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: SldprtNet是一个包含24.2万个工业零件的大规模多模态CAD数据集，支持语义驱动的三维建模与跨模态学习，提供STEP/Sldprt格式3D模型、参数化文本表示、七视图合成图像及人工校验的自然语言描述，并验证了多模态输入对CAD生成任务的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 构建一个面向语义驱动CAD建模和几何深度学习的大规模、高质量、多模态工业零件数据集，解决现有数据集在规模、模态多样性、参数化表达及真实工业适用性方面的不足。

Method: 开发SldprtNet数据集，包括242,000+真实工业零件；设计支持13种CAD命令的编解码器实现3D模型与结构化文本的无损转换；生成七视角合成图像以压缩视觉输入；利用Qwen2.5-VL-7B模型生成并人工校验自然语言描述；开展图像+文本vs纯文本的微调对比实验。

Result: 成功构建首个大规模、全对齐（3D模型/参数脚本/渲染图/自然语言描述）、支持可扩展参数建模的多模态CAD数据集；实验证明图像+文本输入显著优于纯文本输入，验证了多模态数据对CAD生成任务的关键价值。

Conclusion: SldprtNet填补了工业级多模态CAD数据集的空白，为语义驱动建模、几何深度学习和跨模态大模型训练提供了坚实基础，其设计范式（参数化编码+多视图图像+人工对齐描述）具有可推广性。

Abstract: We introduce SldprtNet, a large-scale dataset comprising over 242,000 industrial parts, designed for semantic-driven CAD modeling, geometric deep learning, and the training and fine-tuning of multimodal models for 3D design. The dataset provides 3D models in both .step and .sldprt formats to support diverse training and testing. To enable parametric modeling and facilitate dataset scalability, we developed supporting tools, an encoder and a decoder, which support 13 types of CAD commands and enable lossless transformation between 3D models and a structured text representation. Additionally, each sample is paired with a composite image created by merging seven rendered views from different viewpoints of the 3D model, effectively reducing input token length and accelerating inference. By combining this image with the parameterized text output from the encoder, we employ the lightweight multimodal language model Qwen2.5-VL-7B to generate a natural language description of each part's appearance and functionality. To ensure accuracy, we manually verified and aligned the generated descriptions, rendered images, and 3D models. These descriptions, along with the parameterized modeling scripts, rendered images, and 3D model files, are fully aligned to construct SldprtNet. To assess its effectiveness, we fine-tuned baseline models on a dataset subset, comparing image-plus-text inputs with text-only inputs. Results confirm the necessity and value of multimodal datasets for CAD generation. It features carefully selected real-world industrial parts, supporting tools for scalable dataset expansion, diverse modalities, and ensured diversity in model complexity and geometric features, making it a comprehensive multimodal dataset built for semantic-driven CAD modeling and cross-modal learning.

</details>


### [313] [Evaluating VLMs' Spatial Reasoning Over Robot Motion: A Step Towards Robot Planning with Motion Preferences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13100)
*Wenxi Wu,Jingjing Zhang,Martim Brandão*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文评估了四种视觉语言模型（VLMs）在机器人运动空间推理任务中的能力，发现Qwen2.5-VL表现最佳（零样本71.4%，微调后75%），而GPT-4o表现较差；研究涵盖物体邻近性与路径风格两类运动偏好，并权衡了准确率与计算开销（token数）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基础模型虽已用于任务规划，但其在满足用户空间约束（如距离、拓扑、运动风格）方面的空间推理能力尚不明确，亟需系统评估。

Method: 采用四种查询方法，对四个前沿VLMs进行空间推理能力评测，涵盖物体邻近性和路径风格两类运动偏好，并分析准确率与token消耗的权衡。

Result: Qwen2.5-VL在最优查询方法下零样本准确率达71.4%，微调后达75%；GPT-4o性能更低；验证了VLMs在机器人运动规划中具备一定集成潜力。

Conclusion: VLMs（尤其是Qwen2.5-VL）展现出一定的空间推理能力，有望融入机器人运动规划流程，但性能仍受限，需进一步优化查询策略与模型适配。

Abstract: Understanding user instructions and object spatial relations in surrounding environments is crucial for intelligent robot systems to assist humans in various tasks. The natural language and spatial reasoning capabilities of Vision-Language Models (VLMs) have the potential to enhance the generalization of robot planners on new tasks, objects, and motion specifications. While foundation models have been applied to task planning, it is still unclear the degree to which they have the capability of spatial reasoning required to enforce user preferences or constraints on motion, such as desired distances from objects, topological properties, or motion style preferences. In this paper, we evaluate the capability of four state-of-the-art VLMs at spatial reasoning over robot motion, using four different querying methods. Our results show that, with the highest-performing querying method, Qwen2.5-VL achieves 71.4% accuracy zero-shot and 75% on a smaller model after fine-tuning, and GPT-4o leads to lower performance. We evaluate two types of motion preferences (object-proximity and path-style), and we also analyze the trade-off between accuracy and computation cost in number of tokens. This work shows some promise in the potential of VLM integration with robot motion planning pipelines.

</details>


### [314] [A Feasibility-Enhanced Control Barrier Function Method for Multi-UAV Collision Avoidance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13103)
*Qishen Zhong,Junlong Wu,Jian Yang,Guanwei Xiao,Junqi Wu,Zimeng Jiang,Pingan Fang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种可行性增强的控制屏障函数（FECBF）框架，通过分析CBF约束的内部兼容性并引入符号一致性约束，缓解多无人机密集场景下CBF-QP的不可行性问题，并在仿真与实机实验中验证了其有效性与鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在密集多无人机场景中，多个CBF约束之间可能存在内部不兼容，导致CBF二次规划（CBF-QP）不可行，影响碰撞规避性能。

Method: 分析CBF约束的内部兼容性，推导出内部兼容的充分条件；引入符号一致性约束以缓解不兼容性；将其融入基于最坏情况估计和松弛变量的去中心化CBF-QP中。

Result: 仿真表明该方法显著降低CBF-QP不可行率，提升密集场景下的避碰性能；时延变化下的仿真验证了鲁棒性；真实无人机实验验证了实际可行性。

Conclusion: 所提出的FECBF框架有效提升了CBF-QP在密集多无人机系统中的可行性与避碰性能，兼具理论严谨性与工程实用性。

Abstract: This paper presents a feasibility-enhanced control barrier function (FECBF) framework for multi-UAV collision avoidance. In dense multi-UAV scenarios, the feasibility of the CBF quadratic program (CBF-QP) can be compromised due to internal incompatibility among multiple CBF constraints. To address this issue, we analyze the internal compatibility of CBF constraints and derive a sufficient condition for internal compatibility. Based on this condition, a sign-consistency constraint is introduced to mitigate internal incompatibility. The proposed constraint is incorporated into a decentralized CBF-QP formulation using worst-case estimates and slack variables. Simulation results demonstrate that the proposed method significantly reduces infeasibility and improves collision avoidance performance compared with existing baselines in dense scenarios. Additional simulations under varying time delays demonstrate the robustness of the proposed method. Real-world experiments validate the practical applicability of the proposed method.

</details>


### [315] [Panoramic Multimodal Semantic Occupancy Prediction for Quadruped Robots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13108)
*Guoqiang Zhao,Zhe Yang,Sheng Wu,Fei Teng,Mengfei Duan,Yuanfan Zheng,Kai Luo,Kailun Yang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了首个面向四足机器人的全景多模态占用预测数据集PanoMMOcc，并设计了专用于腿部移动和球面成像的VoxelHound框架，包含垂直抖动补偿（VJC）和多模态信息提示融合（MIPF）模块，在PanoMMOcc上达到SOTA性能（mIoU提升4.16%）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有占用预测方法主要面向轮式自动驾驶，严重依赖RGB线索，在复杂环境中鲁棒性不足，难以适配四足机器人在动态运动下的全景感知需求。

Method: 提出PanoMMOcc数据集与VoxelHound框架；VoxelHound包含两个核心模块：(i) 垂直抖动补偿（VJC）模块以缓解运动中俯仰/翻滚引起的视角扰动；(ii) 多模态信息提示融合（MIPF）模块联合利用全景视觉与辅助模态提升体素占用预测。

Result: VoxelHound在PanoMMOcc数据集上mIoU提升4.16%，达到当前最优性能；同时构建了系统性基准与详尽数据分析。

Conclusion: 该工作填补了四足机器人全景多模态3D占用感知的研究空白，通过新数据集、新方法与公开资源推动具身智能系统的感知发展。

Abstract: Panoramic imagery provides holistic 360° visual coverage for perception in quadruped robots. However, existing occupancy prediction methods are mainly designed for wheeled autonomous driving and rely heavily on RGB cues, limiting their robustness in complex environments. To bridge this gap, (1) we present PanoMMOcc, the first real-world panoramic multimodal occupancy dataset for quadruped robots, featuring four sensing modalities across diverse scenes. (2) We propose a panoramic multimodal occupancy perception framework, VoxelHound, tailored for legged mobility and spherical imaging. Specifically, we design (i) a Vertical Jitter Compensation (VJC) module to mitigate severe viewpoint perturbations caused by body pitch and roll during mobility, enabling more consistent spatial reasoning, and (ii) an effective Multimodal Information Prompt Fusion (MIPF) module that jointly leverages panoramic visual cues and auxiliary modalities to enhance volumetric occupancy prediction. (3) We establish a benchmark based on PanoMMOcc and provide detailed data analysis to enable systematic evaluation of perception methods under challenging embodied scenarios. Extensive experiments demonstrate that VoxelHound achieves state-of-the-art performance on PanoMMOcc (+4.16%} in mIoU). The dataset and code will be publicly released to facilitate future research on panoramic multimodal 3D perception for embodied robotic systems at https://github.com/SXDR/PanoMMOcc, along with the calibration tools released at https://github.com/losehu/CameraLiDAR-Calib.

</details>


### [316] [DecoVLN: Decoupling Observation, Reasoning, and Correction for Vision-and-Language Navigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13133)
*Zihao Xin,Wentong Li,Yixuan Jiang,Bin Wang,Runming Cong,Jie Qin,Shengjun Huang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出DecoVLN框架，通过自适应长时记忆构建和状态-动作对级纠偏微调策略，提升视觉-语言导航在长时程任务中的鲁棒性与准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉-语言导航方法面临长时记忆构建困难和误差累积两大挑战。

Method: 1）将长时记忆构建建模为优化问题，引入自适应精炼机制，基于语义相关性、视觉多样性与时间覆盖性三准则联合评分筛选历史帧；2）提出基于状态-动作对的纠偏微调策略，利用测地距离量化轨迹偏差，在可信区域内采集高质量数据并过滤低质量数据。

Result: 实验表明DecoVLN显著提升导航性能，并已部署于真实环境。

Conclusion: DecoVLN通过优化记忆机制与闭环纠偏策略，有效缓解了长时程VLN中的误差累积与记忆失效问题，增强了实际部署的鲁棒性与稳定性。

Abstract: Vision-and-Language Navigation (VLN) requires agents to follow long-horizon instructions and navigate complex 3D environments. However, existing approaches face two major challenges: constructing an effective long-term memory bank and overcoming the compounding errors problem. To address these issues, we propose DecoVLN, an effective framework designed for robust streaming perception and closed-loop control in long-horizon navigation. First, we formulate long-term memory construction as an optimization problem and introduce adaptive refinement mechanism that selects frames from a historical candidate pool by iteratively optimizing a unified scoring function. This function jointly balances three key criteria: semantic relevance to the instruction, visual diversity from the selected memory, and temporal coverage of the historical trajectory. Second, to alleviate compounding errors, we introduce a state-action pair-level corrective finetuning strategy. By leveraging geodesic distance between states to precisely quantify deviation from the expert trajectory, the agent collects high-quality state-action pairs in the trusted region while filtering out the polluted data with low relevance. This improves both the efficiency and stability of error correction. Extensive experiments demonstrate the effectiveness of DecoVLN, and we have deployed it in real-world environments.

</details>
